# Claude Code - subagents/agent-aaa8fe2220190f82b

**Source**: claude-code/subagents/agent-aaa8fe2220190f82b.jsonl

## USER (2026-07-20 10:23:23)

I need to design an implementation plan for adding chunked prefill support to vllm-neuron, working within the existing NxDI (neuronx_distributed_inference) framework.

## Background Context

The user wants to implement chunked prefill for vllm-neuron. Here's the current state:

### Architecture Overview

**vllm_neuron** is a plugin for vLLM that adds AWS Neuron (Inferentia/Trainium) hardware support. It depends on **NxDI (neuronx_distributed_inference)** as the underlying model execution library.

Key files (all under `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/`):
- `vllm_neuron/platform.py` - Platform config, currently disables chunked prefill at line 397
- `vllm_neuron/core/scheduler.py` - Custom `ContinuousBatchingNeuronScheduler` that prioritizes prefill over decode
- `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_runner.py` - The model runner, already has full chunked prefill input preparation code (`_prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs`, `_process_new_request_for_chunked_prefill`, `_finalize_chunked_prefill_inputs`)
- `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` - Model loading, already handles `chunked_prefill_config` in `_get_default_neuron_config`
- `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` line 3054-3055 - **THE BLOCKER**: `raise NotImplementedError("Chunked Prefill is not available in NxDI for now")`
- `neuronx_distributed_inference/models/config.py` - `ChunkedPrefillConfig` class, NeuronConfig with `is_chunked_prefill` field
- `neuronx_distributed_inference/modules/autobucketing.py` - `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte` already implemented
- `neuronx_distributed_inference/modules/kvcache/block_kv_cache_manager.py` - Block KV cache already has `_init_kv_shape_for_chunked_prefill` and `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill`

### How Chunked Prefill Works on Neuron (Design Already in Code)

1. **CTE model compiled with batch_size=1**: All requests in a chunk are concatenated along the sequence dimension into one "mega-sequence"
2. **Block KV layout required**: Uses paged attention with `slot_mapping` and `block_tables`
3. **2D bucketing for CTE**: buckets on [chunk_size, num_tiles] dimensions
4. **Tile-based attention**: Uses `kernel_q_tile_size` (default 128) and `kernel_kv_tile_size` (default 1024) 
5. **`prefill_completion_state` tensor**: Boolean per-request indicating if prefill is done; incomplete requests get masked logits
6. **Separate TKG model optional**: The `tkg_model_enabled` flag in ChunkedPrefillConfig decides if a separate decode-only model is compiled

### The Single Blocker

In `model_base.py:3054-3055`:
```python
if self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill:
    raise NotImplementedError("Chunked Prefill is not available in NxDI for now")
```

This raises BEFORE `enable_context_encoding()` and `enable_token_generation()` are called. If removed, the model compilation flow would proceed to:
1. Call `enable_context_encoding()` which sets `n_active_tokens = max_context_length` (which = chunk_size when chunked prefill is on)
2. Call `generate_buckets_for_cte()` → `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte()` (already implemented)
3. The block KV cache manager already has chunked prefill initialization code

### What Needs to Happen

The `NotImplementedError` exists because there's likely missing attention kernel support or an untested code path in the NxDI model forward pass for chunked prefill. We need to:

1. Remove or bypass the `NotImplementedError` in NxDI
2. Ensure the model compilation flow works correctly for chunked prefill (CTE with batch_size=1, 2D bucketing)
3. Possibly implement the chunked attention kernel path in NxDI (or find if it already exists but is gated)
4. Enable the vllm_neuron scheduler path (either adapt the custom scheduler or use `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1`)
5. Test the end-to-end flow

### Additional Context from the `NeuronCausalLM.forward()` in model_loader.py

The forward path already handles chunked prefill logit extraction:
```python
if self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill:
    assert kwargs.get("prefill_completion_state") is not None
    idx_for_sampling = kwargs["prefill_completion_state"].nonzero().flatten()
    output = output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]
else:
    output = output.logits[:, -1, :]
```

### The `is_context_encoding` Detection

In `model_base.py:3348`:
```python
is_context_encoding = input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and not position_ids.min().item()
```

For chunked prefill, inputs are concatenated with batch_size=1, so `input_ids.shape[-1]` will be > 1 for both prefill chunks AND decode tokens mixed together. The `position_ids.min()` check might not work correctly when decode tokens (which have position > 0) are mixed in. This detection logic may need adjustment.

### Constraints

- Cannot compile NxDI from source (it's a preinstalled package) — we need to monkey-patch or subclass
- Neuron models require static shapes — all inputs padded to bucket boundaries
- The model runner already has all the input preparation code for chunked prefill
- We're targeting the vLLM V1 scheduler with chunked prefill enabled

Design an implementation plan for enabling chunked prefill in this system. Consider:
1. How to bypass the NotImplementedError (monkey-patch at model load time?)
2. Whether to use the vLLM native scheduler or modify the custom neuron scheduler
3. What changes are needed in the NxDI model's forward path for correct CTE/TKG dispatch
4. How to handle the is_context_encoding detection for chunked prefill mixed batches
5. What compile-time configuration is needed (ChunkedPrefillConfig, batch sizes, block sizes)
6. What testing/verification approach to use

[{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_01TuiyNugjfdqRBgc2YGJ5Ls', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': '101\tdef generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte(inference_config: InferenceConfig):\n102\t    """\n103\t    Generate buckets for chunked prefill context encoding model\n104\t\n105\t    It has two bucketing dimensions:\n106\t        - chunk size: how many new tokens to process per iteration\n107\t        - number of tiles: how many tiles to compute for attention per iteration\n108\t\n109\t    Chunked prefill in NxDI splits attention computation with a tile grid, and\n110\t    the tile size is defined by `kernel_q_tile_size` and `kernel_kv_tile_size`.\n111\t\n112\t    For example, if the chunks size=256, max_len=1024, max_num_seqs=8,\n113\t    kernel_q_tile_size=128, kernel_kv_tile_size=512, the max number of tiles\n114\t    needed will be (256/128) * (8*1024/512) = 2 * 16 = 32. Since not all the\n115\t    tiles are needed by the final result, it has a bucketing dimension on the\n116\t    number of tiles.\n117\t    """\n118\t    neuron_config = inference_config.neuron_config\n119\t    chunked_prefill_config = neuron_config.chunked_prefill_config\n120\t    max_context_length = neuron_config.max_context_length\n121\t    assert chunked_prefill_config is not None\n122\t\n123\t    q_tile_size = chunked_prefill_config.kernel_q_tile_size\n124\t    kv_tile_size = chunked_prefill_config.kernel_kv_tile_size\n125\t\n126\t    max_q_len = max_context_length\n127\t    max_kv_cache_len = neuron_config.max_length * chunked_prefill_config.max_num_seqs\n128\t    max_num_tiles = ceil(max_q_len / q_tile_size) * ceil(max_kv_cache_len / kv_tile_size)\n129\t\n130\t    if not neuron_config.enable_bucketing:\n131\t        return [[max_context_length, max_num_tiles]]\n132\t    elif neuron_config.context_encoding_buckets is not None:\n133\t        return neuron_config.context_encoding_buckets\n134\t\n135\t    # [{'tool_use_id': 'toolu_bdrk_01AZcCCnYEczwM1r6wh3R7aY', 'type': 'tool_result', 'content': '150\t    def _get_block_cache_and_reshape_bhsd(self, cache: Tensor, active_block_table: Tensor):\n151\t        """\n152\t        Reorder the cache based on the table indices from active_block_table, and return\n153\t        them in BHSD layout.\n154\t\n155\t        This is for prefix caching only.\n156\t\n157\t        Args:\n158\t            cache: cache in block layout. Non-tiled:\n159\t                (max_blocks, num_heads_per_rank, block_size, head_dimension).\n160\t                Tiled (5D, only when attn_block_tkg_nki_kernel_enabled=False):\n161\t                (max_blocks, tiling_factor, block_size//tiling_factor, num_heads_per_rank, head_dimension).\n162\t            active_block_table: indices of precomputed cache blocks in shape (batch_size, max_blocks_per_seq)\n163\t\n164\t        Returns:\n165\t            cache: reordered cache in BHSD layout\n166\t        """\n167\t        if self.block_tiling:\n168\t            batch_size, _ = active_block_table.shape\n169\t            _, _, num_block_tiles, num_heads_per_rank, head_dimension = cache.shape\n170\t            cache_reshaped = cache.reshape(-1, num_block_tiles, num_heads_per_rank, head_dimension)\n171\t            index_array = active_block_table.reshape(-1) * self.block_tiling_factor\n172\t            index_array = index_array.unsqueeze(-1) + torch.arange(self.block_tiling_factor)\n173\t            selected_cache = cache_reshaped.index_select(\n174\t                dim=0, index=index_array.reshape(-1)\n175\t            ).reshape(batch_size, -1, num_heads_per_rank, head_dimension)\n176\t            return selected_cache.permute((0, 2, 1, 3))  # BSHD to BHSD\n177\t\n178\t        # Non-tiled prefix-caching layout matches chunked-prefill TKG; reuse helper.\n179\t        return self._get_cache_for_chunked_prefill(\n180\t            cache, active_block_table, is_for_context_encoding=False\n181\t        )\n182\t\n183\t    def _get_cache_for_chunked_prefill(\n184\t        self,\n185\t        cache: Tensor,\n186\t        active_block_table: Tensor,\n187\t        is_for_context_encoding: bool\n188\t    ):\n189\t        """\n190\t        Read KV cache for chunked prefill.\n191\t\n192\t        For CTE, it return the whole cache as it is. For TKG, it selects\n193\t        specific KV cache based on the block table, and reshape into bhsd\n194\t        before returning.\n195\t        """\n196\t        # CTE usecase\n197\t        if is_for_context_encoding:\n198\t            return cache\n199\t\n200\t        # TKG usecase\n201\t        batch_size, _ = active_block_table.shape\n202\t        num_blocks, num_heads_per_rank, block_size, head_dimension = cache.shape\n203\t\n204\t        cache = cache.reshape(num_blocks * num_heads_per_rank, block_size * head_dimension)\n205\t\n206\t        indices = ## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:32:17)

[{'type': 'thinking', 'thinking': "This is important. The `CHUNKED_ATTENTION_SUPPORTED_NEURON_CONFIG` is for **chunked attention** (which is a different feature from chunked prefill!). Chunked attention is about splitting the attention computation into chunks during CTE, while chunked prefill is about splitting the prefill across multiple iterations. The config says `is_chunked_prefill: False` meaning that if you're using chunked attention AND chunked prefill together, it will fail validation. But this only fires when `attention_chunk_size < seq_len`.\n\nNow let me look at the scheduler:", 'signature': 'EvYFCmUIDxABGAIqQNYmfaSBJPPsdljpJfMt3jGTmtfFHOqIN9B12cXbXriWcvFoaBMjxOdk0a/4PuZult3belbZCt0oeRQJrE/DztgyD2NsYXVkZS1vcHVzLTQtNjgAQgh0aGlua2luZxIMEVrj7MZHY6dS8sREGgzw/4Ete0HPKblu1R8iMIxOIJqFE09qFQvSz6Lixq5VCpqMfVtE4mV+Hkj+DukpvqWw1iavIZRAl7rY0TuJiyq+BLyXubTNHZciN1QQYpihjd3IehqCPwi231fSAoKgOE3eryiV+dhspZQwBIJiK92Kj4fsPOlON/xFPECv4f1nNjosYVXuN4ynHSMz1Wz1ClgfdR+VAPSnql7NX3V2T2Ie5tzyeee4HnITwOAzsOu5sXg0+4ijAxujUV1U5zMSpnHUXKvMuapDzod8GHkMnFODqjpQtdxc1Aml7cVhdEYx0aWlbzF6YFje0DJZGZW9jKozwxhaMNtqZvNYgKXHTL7KXG2jeLlUfuaMYnN5qxwZDi0OJf+q+sPSOoFvLX+6x9+9Fh2s9NXmRHxgoL4CKva2YStis2TwqJFm/PDmIPtCJlFPKbAav/TUr2O8yJW9iX3qT2ARPD6+SYgpBFCgNDK+8HujGF0dKJd89qBKRVKQMOhYUupLAoLJfWYe/VU9Az5dmJj8YUutS6Bxf7cOb5VDPHDnQxReQuhn0KIsTlPcclC2VSOYAe1eeZYSs6VEI9XTkbqi+Hrpl8njJ4Pt3jNBL5vGAsyz269mXjmmNW4LywhfpCrWvFQEVIUUJk7SGrAdg1v/8UuFS65cMoaZHN2Pc0qnd26fWu1va1VQAWJm7bSrEMr0VAYUtzwOpMVa6kXSg0TP3Idm3AdoS7CQFM7d7grX8p6EZRsh0nbdjuGtEDTHaD63LV2OC7udhODwkqsE++EemJUkXov/Pxt/VK86Dz1n/FSxjDrTmaYXCfcDmAdV8AOA2Kfb87IW8rnPzVx4uSzClJUXlVN2kctpzugYAQ=='}]

[{'type': 'text', 'text': 'This is another critical finding. At line 974, for CTE (context encoding) with right padding, the model takes `torch.max(position_ids)` to extract the hidden state at the last active token. For chunked prefill, there are MULTIPLE requests concatenated in the sequence dimension (batch_size=1), and we need hidden states for EACH request\'s last token, not just the overall last token.\n\nThe `NeuronCausalLM.forward()` in the vllm_neuron layer handles this at line 548-553 by:\n```python\nif self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill:\n    idx_for_sampling = kwargs["prefill_completion_state"].nonzero().flatten()\n    output = output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]\n```\n\nThis means the NxDI model must return ALL logits (not just the last-token logit) when chunked prefill is enabled. ## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:38:50)

[{'type': 'thinking', 'thinking': "Now I have a very thorough understanding of the architecture. Let me trace through the key issues:\n\n1. **The NotImplementedError** at `model_base.py:3054-3055` - this is the single blocker that prevents the rest of the (already implemented) code from executing.\n\n2. **The `is_context_encoding` detection** at `model_base.py:3348`:\n   ```python\n   is_context_encoding = input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and not position_ids.min().item()\n   ```\n   For chunked prefill with batch_size=1, input_ids will be `[1, chunk_size]` where chunk_size > 1. \n\nThe position_ids array contains all positions for the concatenated prefill and decode tokens. If the chunk starts at position 0 (the first chunk), `position_ids.min()` will be 0 and `is_context_encoding` becomes true. But if the chunk begins at a later position or contains only decode tokens, `position_ids.min()` will be greater than 0, making `is_context_encoding` false.\n\nThis creates a routing problem: the CTE model should always handle chunked prefill since it processes both prefill and decode tokens together, but the current logic might incorrectly route decode-only batches to the TKG model when all positions are greater than 0. The TKG model is optional and shouldn't be used for these cases. The dispatch logic in `_get_model_outputs()` checks whether the input sequence length is greater than 1 and whether position IDs start from 0. For chunked prefill batches with shape `[1, chunk_size]`, the sequence length check always passes, so the routing between CTE and TKG models hinges entirely on the position IDs value.\n\nThen there's a critical mismatch in how hidden states are handled: the NxDI model slices hidden states based on the maximum position for chunked prefill, but the vllm_neuron layer expects the full sequence logits to be available when sampling. This means either `output_logits` must be enabled or the hidden state slicing logic needs to be bypassed depending on the `sliced_hidden` configuration. The `output_logits` flag at line 1018 adds the full logits to the output, but by that point the hidden states have already been sliced down to `[B, 1, vocab]` at line 976, so it's still only returning logits for a single token rather than the full chunk needed for chunked prefill operations. The chunk size will be much larger than 1 and won't match the speculation length, so the gather operation will execute. There's an additional check for windowed context encoding that also skips the gather, but for chunked prefill we need to bypass this entirely with a monkey-patch to get all logits back. In `NeuronCausalLM.forward()`, when on-device sampling is configured it returns hidden states, otherwise for chunked prefill it samples from a specific position in the logits.\n\nThe issue is that chunked prefill needs on-device sampling disabled to work properly, but the default config enables it with dynamic sampling. This creates a conflict — either we disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill, or we need to modify the on-device sampling path to handle chunked prefill by knowing which positions to sample from.\n\nSince we can't modify the NxDI source code, the strategy is to monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` to bypass the NotImplementedError and proceed with enabling context encoding, then fix the `is_context_encoding` detection logic in `_get_model_outputs` to properly handle chunked prefill scenarios.\n\nWe also need to patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` to skip the hidden state slicing that normally extracts only the final position, since chunked prefill requires logits for all sequence positions so vllm_neuron can select the correct ones. Finally, on-device sampling should be disabled for chunked prefill operations.\n\nTo make this work with the scheduler, we need to set `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` to use vLLM's native V1 scheduler instead of the custom neuron scheduler which explicitly blocks chunked prefill. ## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:39:00)

[{'type': 'text', 'text': "This is important: the default config always sets `on_device_sampling_config`. When on_device_sampling is used, the model returns sampled tokens directly (via `output.hidden_states`). When it's NOT used (chunked prefill path), logits are returned via `output.logits`. \n\nFor chunked prefill, the critical issue is that `output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]` needs ALL position logits to be present (not just the last token). This means `output_logits=True` must be set, OR the NxDI model must NOT perform the hidden_states slicing at line 964-976.\n\nLet me check what happens in the on_device_sampling code path for chunked prefill. On line 540-546, when `on_device_sampling_config` is set, it directly uses `output.hidden_states`. So for chunked prefill with on-device sampling, the sampler runs on device, and we do not need the full logits. But on line 547-555, when on_device_sampling is NOT configured, we need `output.logits` to contain ALL positions' logits.\n\nGiven that the default config always uses `on_device_sampling_config`, I suspect the chunked prefill path is designed to work WITHOUT on_device_sampling. Let me double-check:"}]

It generates limited number of buckets, to avoid\n75\t    resulting in too many buckets when combining with other bucketing\n76\t    dimensions.\n77\t\n78\t    This design on the bucketing is based on experience, and it is\n79\t    subject to changes in future.\n80\t    """\n81\t    if max_context_len < q_tile_size:\n82\t        return [q_tile_size]\n83\t\n84\t    num_q_tiles = ceil(max_context_len / q_tile_size)\n85\t\n86\t    all_buckets = list(range(1, num_q_tiles + 1))\n87\t    all_buckets = [b * q_tile_size for b in all_buckets]\n88\t\n89\t    left_index = 0\n90\t    right_index = len(all_buckets) - 1\n91\t    median_index = right_index // 2\n92\t\n93\t    chunk_size_buckets = [all_buckets[left_index]]\n94\t    if median_index > left_index:\n95\t        chunk_size_buckets.append(all_buckets[median_index])\n96\t    if right_index > median_index:\n97\t        chunk_size_buckets.append(all_buckets[right_index])\n98\t    return chunk_size_buckets\n99\t\n100\t\n101\tdef generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte(inference_config: InferenceConfig):\n102\t    """\n103\t    Generate buckets for chunked prefill context encoding model\n104\t'}]

## ASSISTANT (2026-07-20 10:42:09)

[{'type': 'text', 'text': 'Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the entire codebase. Let me assemble the implementation plan.\n\n---\n\n## Implementation Plan: Chunked Prefill Support for vllm-neuron\n\n### Executive Summary\n\nChunked prefill has extensive scaffolding already implemented across both vllm_neuron and NxDI. The vllm_neuron model runner has complete input preparation code. NxDI has the bucket generation, KV cache initialization, and configuration plumbing. The single hard blocker is a `NotImplementedError` at NxDI `model_base.py:3054-3055`. However, simply removing that raises exposes three deeper issues that must also be resolved:\n\n1. **Model dispatch in `_get_model_outputs`** -- the method only passes `slot_mapping`/`block_table` to the CTE model in the `is_prefix_caching` branch; the plain `_is_prefill` branch does not, which breaks block KV writes\n2. **Hidden state slicing** -- at `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` line 964-976, the model extracts only a single hidden state (at `max(position_ids)`), discarding the full-sequence logits that chunked prefill needs\n3. **Input generator for compilation** -- `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` has no chunked prefill branch, so the model cannot be traced with the correct input signature (including `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, etc.)\n\nSince NxDI is a preinstalled package and cannot be recompiled, all fixes must be applied as monkey-patches from the vllm_neuron layer.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 1: Bypass the NotImplementedError\n\n**Approach**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` before model instantiation.\n\n**Where to patch**: In `vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py`, inside `_load_weights_common` (around line 187), BEFORE the model class is instantiated.\n\n**Implementation**:\n```python\n# At the top of _load_weights_common or in a helper function\nfrom neuronx_distributed_inference.models.model_base import NeuronBaseForCausalLM\n\n_original_nxdi_init = NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__\n\ndef _patched_nxdi_init(self, *args, **kwargs):\n    # Temporarily disable the NotImplementedError guard\n    # Save the is_chunked_prefill state, set to False, call init, restore\n    # OR: patch with a version that skips the check and continues to enable_context_encoding/enable_token_generation\n    _original_nxdi_init(self, *args, **kwargs)\n\n# The cleaner approach: patch only the specific check\n```\n\nA cleaner pattern is to subclass. Since the vllm_neuron layer already instantiates models through `neuronx_model_cls(...)`, we can create a wrapper that intercepts initialization. However, the simplest reliable approach is:\n\n**Strategy A (Preferred)**: Before calling the NxDI model constructor, monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` to replace the `NotImplementedError` block with the proper initialization logic:\n\n```python\ndef _chunked_prefill_init_patch(original_init):\n    def patched_init(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        # Store the flag before original init\n        # The original init raises if is_chunked_prefill is True\n        # We need to bypass that and instead do what the code AFTER the raise does\n        \n        # Option: temporarily patch neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = False,\n        # call original_init, then restore and call enable_context_encoding + enable_token_generation manually\n        ...\n    return patched_init\n```\n\n**Strategy B (More surgical)**: Since the `NotImplementedError` occurs between `self.model_wrapper = self.get_model_wrapper_cls()` (line 3052) and `self.enable_context_encoding()` (line 3062), we can:\n1. Temporarily set `neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = False` in the config\n2. Call the original init (which will skip the check and proceed normally to `enable_context_encoding` + `enable_token_generation`)\n3. After init, restore `neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill = True`\n\nBut this is incorrect because `enable_context_encoding` needs `is_chunked_prefill=True` to generate the correct 2D buckets via `generate_buckets_for_cte` -> `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte`.\n\n**Strategy C (Best)**: Patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` to skip ONLY the `NotImplementedError` raise. Replace the method such that lines 3054-3055 are simply omitted. The rest of `__init__` already does the right thing: it calls `enable_context_encoding()` and then `enable_token_generation()` (or skips TKG if `tkg_model_enabled=False` in ChunkedPrefillConfig).\n\nWait -- examining line 3057-3068, after the `NotImplementedError` would have been raised, the code continues with:\n```python\nif self.neuron_config.enable_fused_speculation:\n    ...\nelse:\n    self.enable_context_encoding()\n    if self.neuron_config.speculation_length > 0:\n        self.enable_speculation()\n    elif ...:\n        ...\n    else:\n        self.enable_token_generation()\n```\n\nFor chunked prefill:\n- CTE model: `enable_context_encoding()` will set `n_active_tokens = max_context_length` (= chunk_size) and call `generate_buckets_for_cte()` which dispatches to `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte()`\n- TKG model: `enable_token_generation()` will create the separate decode model (only if `tkg_model_enabled=True` in ChunkedPrefillConfig)\n\nThe correct patch is to JUST skip the raise. If we use the `tkg_model_enabled=False` path, only the CTE model is compiled (all requests including decodes go through CTE).\n\n---\n\n### Phase 2: Fix Model Dispatch in `_get_model_outputs`\n\n**Problem**: When `is_prefix_caching=False` and `is_chunked_prefill=True`, the method enters `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids):` at line 3632, which calls `context_encoding_model(input_ids, attention_mask, position_ids, seq_ids, sampling_params, prev_hidden, adapter_ids, *llava_args)` -- WITHOUT passing `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `full_context_lens`, or `computed_context_lens`.\n\n**Why this matters**: The block KV cache manager\'s `update_cache` method needs `slot_mapping` to write new KV entries. The `get_cache` method needs `active_block_table` to read KV entries. Without these, the model will fail during attention computation.\n\n**Solution**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs` to add a chunked prefill dispatch branch BEFORE the `elif self._is_prefill(position_ids)` check.\n\nThe chunked prefill dispatch should:\n1. Always route to `context_encoding_model` (since batch_size=1, all inputs are concatenated into one "mega-sequence")\n2. Pass `slot_mapping`, `block_table` (as `active_block_table`), `full_context_lens`, and `computed_context_lens`\n3. Compute `num_queries = full_context_lens - computed_context_lens`\n\nThe input signature for the CTE model with block KV follows the `is_prefix_caching` pattern:\n```python\noutputs = self.context_encoding_model(\n    input_ids,\n    attention_mask,\n    position_ids,\n    seq_ids,\n    sampling_params,\n    torch.empty(0),  # prev_hidden\n    adapter_ids,\n    torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0), torch.empty(0),  # placeholders\n    slot_mapping,\n    block_table,\n    num_queries,\n    computed_context_lens,\n)\n```\n\nHowever, this input signature must EXACTLY match what the compiled model expects. Since we cannot recompile, the input_generator must also be patched for chunked prefill (Phase 5).\n\n**Alternative approach**: Since `is_prefix_caching` and `is_chunked_prefill` share the same block KV infrastructure, set BOTH `is_prefix_caching=True` AND `is_chunked_prefill=True` in the config. This leverages the existing `is_prefix_caching` dispatch path which already passes `slot_mapping` and `block_table`. The `BlockKVCacheManager` already handles the distinction: when `is_chunked_prefill=True`, it uses `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill` which returns the raw cache for CTE and does block-table selection for TKG.\n\nBUT: the config validation at line 308-311 asserts:\n```python\nassert self.is_block_kv_layout, "is_block_kv_layout has to be true for chunked prefill"\n```\nAnd `CHUNKED_ATTENTION_SUPPORTED_NEURON_CONFIG` at line 28 has `is_prefix_caching: False` combined with `is_chunked_prefill: False`, meaning the "chunked attention" (a different feature -- fixed-size attention window for long contexts) does not support either. This is separate from "chunked prefill."\n\nThe conclusion: we CANNOT just set `is_prefix_caching=True` because that triggers a different code path in the KV cache manager (`_get_block_cache_and_reshape_bhsd` instead of `_get_cache_for_chunked_prefill`). We need the monkey-patch approach.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 3: Fix Hidden State / Logit Extraction\n\n**Problem**: At `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` line 964-976, after `get_model_output` returns, the code does:\n```python\nif not self.sliced_hidden:\n    index = torch.max(position_ids, dim=1, keepdim=True).indices\n    hidden_states = torch.gather(hidden_states, dim=1, index=...)\n```\n\nThis extracts only the SINGLE token at max position. For chunked prefill (batch_size=1), we need hidden states for ALL positions because the vllm_neuron layer extracts specific indices via `prefill_completion_state`.\n\n**Solution options**:\n\nOption A: Set `output_logits=True` in the NeuronConfig. When `output_logits=True`, the model returns BOTH the sampled/extracted result AND the full logits tensor (see line 1018-1024). The vllm_neuron layer uses `output.logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]` to extract per-request logits.\n\nBUT: the slicing STILL happens (it happens before `lm_head` and logit computation). The `output_logits` flag causes the full logits to be appended to outputs as a second element, but those logits are computed AFTER `hidden_states` is sliced. So this does not help.\n\nOption B: Disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill AND skip the hidden-state slicing. For chunked prefill, the model should NOT slice hidden_states at all. Instead, it should run lm_head on the full sequence and return all logits. The vllm_neuron layer then selects the appropriate logit positions.\n\nThe hidden_states slicing at line 964-976 occurs inside `NeuronBaseModel.forward()`. For chunked prefill:\n- `self.sliced_hidden` is False (since sequence_parallel is typically disabled for CTE in chunked prefill with batch_size=1)\n- `position_ids.shape[-1]` is the chunk_size (not 1 and not speculation_length)\n- So it WILL enter the slicing branch\n\n**The fix**: Monkey-patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` to skip the slicing when `is_chunked_prefill=True`. OR: more precisely, the issue is that `self._is_context_encoding(input_ids)` returns True for chunked prefill, and the slicing code runs for CTE. We need to either:\n\n1. Make the model NOT slice for chunked prefill, OR\n2. Make the model return full logits for chunked prefill\n\nThe most elegant approach: When `is_chunked_prefill=True`, skip the hidden_state gathering entirely. The `lm_head` runs on `hidden_states` of shape `[1, chunk_size, hidden_dim]` and produces logits of shape `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`. The vllm_neuron layer then extracts `logits[0, idx_for_sampling, :]`.\n\n**BUT**: This has compilation implications. The model is traced with a specific output shape. If we skip the slicing, the output shape changes from `[1, 1, vocab_size]` to `[1, chunk_size, vocab_size]`. This means the compiled model must know at trace time that slicing is skipped.\n\nThis is where the monkey-patching gets complex. Since the model is traced/compiled during `enable_context_encoding()`, the forward method behavior at trace time determines the compiled NEFF. We need to ensure the model is compiled without the slicing.\n\n**Key insight**: The chunked prefill CTE model MUST be compiled with the full-sequence output (no last-token extraction). This means we need to patch `NeuronBaseModel.forward()` BEFORE compilation happens. Since compilation happens inside `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` -> `enable_context_encoding()` -> `model_wrapper.trace()`, we need the patch applied early.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 4: Disable On-Device Sampling for Chunked Prefill CTE\n\n**Problem**: The default config creates `OnDeviceSamplingConfig(dynamic=True, deterministic=False)`. With on-device sampling, the model internally samples tokens and returns them. For chunked prefill, we need raw logits for ALL positions (not just sampled tokens at a single position).\n\n**Solution**: Set `on_device_sampling_config=None` in the neuron config when `enable_chunked_prefill=True`. This is partially addressed already in `_get_default_neuron_config` (the code already sets `batch_size=1` and `max_context_length=max_num_batched_tokens` for chunked prefill). But `on_device_sampling_config` is ALWAYS set.\n\n**Implementation**: In `_get_default_neuron_config`, add:\n```python\nif scheduler_config.enable_chunked_prefill:\n    on_device_sampling_config = None  # Need full logits for all positions\n```\n\nOr alternatively, disable it via the `NEURON_ON_DEVICE_SAMPLING_DISABLED=1` environment variable.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 5: Handle Model Compilation (Input Generator)\n\n**Problem**: `ModelWrapper.input_generator()` does not have a chunked prefill branch. The compiled model needs to accept `slot_mapping`, `block_table`, `num_queries`, `computed_context_lens` as inputs (matching the dispatch call signature).\n\n**Solution**: Monkey-patch `ModelWrapper.input_generator` to handle the chunked prefill case, generating trace inputs that include:\n- `input_ids`: shape `[1, chunk_size]` (batch_size=1)\n- `attention_mask`: shape `[1, chunk_size]`\n- `position_ids`: shape `[1, chunk_size]`\n- `seq_ids`: shape `[1]`\n- `sampling_params`: appropriate shape\n- `prev_hidden`: `torch.empty(0)`\n- `adapter_ids`: shape `[1]`\n- `slot_mapping`: shape `[1, chunk_size]` (for block KV writes)\n- `block_table`: shape `[max_num_seqs, max_blocks_per_seq]` (for KV reads)\n- `num_queries`: shape `[max_num_seqs, 1]` (how many new tokens per request)\n- `computed_context_lens`: shape `[max_num_seqs, 1]` (previously computed context)\n\nThe `input_generator` must produce inputs for EACH bucket. The 2D buckets are `[chunk_size, num_tiles]` pairs from `generate_buckets_for_chunked_prefill_cte`.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 6: Scheduler Configuration\n\n**Approach**: Use `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1` to enable the vLLM V1 native scheduler with chunked prefill.\n\nThe platform.py code at line 381 already handles this:\n```python\nif disable_scheduler_override:\n    # The vLLM V1 native scheduler will be used with chunked prefill enabled.\n    assert vllm_config.cache_config.block_size is not None\n```\n\nThe native V1 scheduler has built-in chunked prefill support and will produce `SchedulerOutput` with `num_scheduled_tokens` per request, mixed prefill+decode batches, etc. The model runner\'s `_prepare_chunked_prefill_inputs` already handles this scheduler output format.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 7: The `is_context_encoding` Detection Problem\n\n**Analysis**: In `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.forward()` at line 3348:\n```python\nis_context_encoding = input_ids.shape[-1] > 1 and not position_ids.min().item()\n```\n\nFor chunked prefill with batch_size=1:\n- `input_ids.shape[-1]` = chunk_size (always > 1)\n- `position_ids.min()` = the minimum position in the concatenated chunk\n\nThe second condition `not position_ids.min().item()` means `position_ids.min() == 0`. In chunked prefill, the chunk always contains at least one request whose first token is at position 0 (a new prefill starting), OR it may contain only decode tokens (where all positions > 0).\n\nWhen the chunk contains ONLY decode tokens (all `position_ids > 0`), `is_context_encoding` will be False. This would incorrectly route to the TKG model. But with chunked prefill (no separate TKG model, `tkg_model_enabled=False`), there IS no TKG model.\n\n**Solution**: When `is_chunked_prefill=True`:\n- Always route to `context_encoding_model` regardless of `is_context_encoding`\n- The CTE model handles both prefill and decode tokens in the same forward pass\n\nThe monkey-patch for `_get_model_outputs` (Phase 2) should handle this by checking `self.neuron_config.is_chunked_prefill` FIRST, before the `is_prefix_caching` or `_is_prefill` checks.\n\n---\n\n### Phase 8: Configuration Requirements\n\nWhen launching with chunked prefill:\n\n```bash\nDISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER=1 \\\nNEURON_ON_DEVICE_SAMPLING_DISABLED=1 \\\npython -m vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server \\\n    --model <model_path> \\\n    --device neuron \\\n    --override-neuron-config \'{"chunked_prefill_config": {"max_num_seqs": 8, "tkg_model_enabled": false, "kernel_q_tile_size": 128, "kernel_kv_tile_size": 1024}}\' \\\n    --block-size 128 \\\n    --max-num-batched-tokens 2048 \\\n    --max-num-seqs 8 \\\n    --num-gpu-blocks-override <calculated>\n```\n\n---\n\n### Implementation Order\n\n1. **Create a chunked prefill patch module**: `/path/to/vllm_neuron/worker/chunked_prefill_patches.py`\n2. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__**: Skip NotImplementedError\n3. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseModel.forward()**: Skip hidden-state slicing for chunked prefill\n4. **Monkey-patch NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs**: Add chunked prefill dispatch branch\n5. **Monkey-patch ModelWrapper.input_generator**: Add chunked prefill input shapes\n6. **Modify `_get_default_neuron_config`**: Disable on-device sampling for chunked prefill\n7. **Apply patches in model loader**: Before model instantiation in `NeuronCausalLM._load_weights_common`\n8. **Testing**: Unit tests for input preparation, integration test with small model\n\n---\n\n### Risks and Mitigations\n\n| Risk | Impact | Mitigation |\n|------|--------|------------|\n| Attention kernel does not support chunked prefill tile patterns | Model compilation fails | The bucket generation code exists and is tested; NKI kernels for block KV are already in place |\n| Full-sequence lm_head causes memory pressure | OOM on large chunk sizes | Limit chunk_size via `max_num_batched_tokens`; use smaller buckets |\n| Monkey-patches break on NxDI version upgrades | Runtime errors | Version-pin NxDI; add defensive checks for method signatures |\n| 2D bucketing creates too many compilation targets | Long compilation time | Limit bucket count in `generate_buckets_on_chunk_size` |\n| Mixed decode+prefill attention mask is incorrect | Wrong outputs | The existing `create_attn_mask` for CTE produces a causal mask along the full concatenated sequence; verify correctness |\n\n---\n\n### Critical Files for Implementation\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_loader.py` -- where monkey-patches must be applied before model instantiation, and where `_get_default_neuron_config` disables on-device sampling for chunked prefill\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_base.py` -- contains the three methods to monkey-patch: `NeuronBaseForCausalLM.__init__` (line 3054), `NeuronBaseModel.forward` (line 964-976), and `NeuronBaseForCausalLM._get_model_outputs` (line 3549)\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/neuronx_distributed_inference/models/model_wrapper.py` -- `ModelWrapper.input_generator` (line 206) needs a chunked prefill trace-input branch\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/worker/neuronx_distributed_model_runner.py` -- already complete chunked prefill input preparation; only minor adjustments needed for on-device-sampling disabled path\n- `/opt/aws_neuronx_venv_pytorch_inference_vllm_0_16/lib/python3.12/site-packages/vllm_neuron/platform.py` -- scheduling configuration (line 349-397); already handles `DISABLE_NEURON_CUSTOM_SCHEDULER`'}]
